  //<![CDATA[
    function loadScript(url, callback) {
      var script = document.createElement("script");
      script.type = "text/javascript";
    
      if (script.readyState) {  //Internet Explorer
          script.onreadystatechange = function() {
            if (script.readyState == "loaded" ||
                    script.readyState == "complete") {
              script.onreadystatechange = null;
              callback();
            }
          };
      } else {  //Other browsers
        script.onload = function() {
          callback();
        };
      }
    
      script.src = url;
      document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
    }
    
    function initAppleId() {
      AppleID.auth.init({
        clientId : 'com.goodreads.app', 
        scope : 'name email',
        redirectURI: 'https://www.goodreads.com/apple_users/sign_in_with_apple_web',
        state: 'apple_oauth_state_ac754766-5cc1-4498-8160-fd59c9c421b8'
      });
    }
    
    var initializeSiwa = function() {
      var APPLE_SIGN_IN_JS_URL =  "https://appleid.cdn-apple.com/appleauth/static/jsapi/appleid/1/en_US/appleid.auth.js"
      loadScript(APPLE_SIGN_IN_JS_URL, initAppleId);
    };

  <span id="freeText1569113700665347948" style="display:none">Anna Latham didn’t know how complicated life could be until she became a werewolf. And until she was mated to Charles Cornick, the son — and enforcer — of Bran, the leader of the North American werewolves, she didn’t know how dangerous it could be either...<br /><br />Anna and Charles have just been enlisted to attend a summit to present Bran’s controversial proposition: that the wolves should finally reveal themselves to humans. But the most feared Alpha in Europe is dead set against the plan — and it seems like someone else might be too. When Anna is attacked by vampires using pack magic, the kind of power only werewolves should be able to draw on, Charles and Anna must combine their talents to hunt down whoever is behind it all — or risk losing everything...</span>

<a href="/questions/761020-i-m-about-to-dive-into-book-2-in-the">I&#39;m about to dive into book #2 in the Alpha and Omega series, but before I do...
Reading the description I have to ask, are most of the Alpha &amp; Omega stories about someone gaining the ability to manipulate pack magic?

Ugh! Vampires.</a>

<div class='answererUserIcon'>
<a class="leftAlignedImage userPhoto" href="/user/show/59109315-rae-whitefeather"><img alt="" src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/users/1472494347i/59109315._UX100_CR0,0,100,100_.jpg" /></a>

<div class='communityAnswerTextContainer'>
<span class='communityAnswererName'>
<a href="/user/show/59109315-rae-whitefeather">Rae Whitefeather</a>

<span class='communityAnswerText'>
<div class='spoiler'>
This answer contains spoilers…
<span class='spoilerAnswerText'>
<a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[
  
    To straight up answer your question, yes. Not all the books in this series have this touch- just these two as far as I'm aware.<br /><br />Also, to be more techni<a href="#" rel="nofollow noopener">…more</a>
    To straight up answer your question, yes. Not all the books in this series have this touch- just these two as far as I'm aware.<br /><br />Also, to be more technical,<br /><br />They don't actually steal the magic, or even really manipulate it. The magic was given to them by, as I like to put it, "the big bad wolf."<a href="#" rel="nofollow noopener">(less)</a>
  
 <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span>
</span>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/821731834?book_show_action=true">Jan 12, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Christy" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Christy" href="/user/show/11284813-christy">Christy</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer821731834" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer3687415504966209750"><a href='http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20Reviews%207/7b517781-eeb8-4066-b91a-a61d25db3695_zpsaeap1oay.jpg.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1432806124i/15007574.jpg' alt=' photo 7b517781-eeb8-4066-b91a-a61d25db3695_zpsaeap1oay.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/>Every once in a while, it feels so good to jump out of the romance genre and jump back into some Urban Fantasy/PNR. Patricia Briggs is one of my go to authors when it comes to these types of books. After listening to the first book in this series (<i>Cry Wolf</i>), I decided to do book 2 in audio as well. I’m happy I did. It was fast listening and the narrator did a great job voicing Anna and Charles. <br/><br/><i>Hunting Ground</i> takes place in Seattle. If you’ve read the Mercy Thompson series, you remember that</span>
  <span id="freeText3687415504966209750" style="display:none"><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20Reviews%207/7b517781-eeb8-4066-b91a-a61d25db3695_zpsaeap1oay.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1432806124i/15007574.jpg" alt=" photo 7b517781-eeb8-4066-b91a-a61d25db3695_zpsaeap1oay.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Every once in a while, it feels so good to jump out of the romance genre and jump back into some Urban Fantasy/PNR. Patricia Briggs is one of my go to authors when it comes to these types of books. After listening to the first book in this series (<i>Cry Wolf</i>), I decided to do book 2 in audio as well. I’m happy I did. It was fast listening and the narrator did a great job voicing Anna and Charles. <br><br><i>Hunting Ground</i> takes place in Seattle. If you’ve read the Mercy Thompson series, you remember that book where the were’s are considering ‘coming out’ to the world- well, the time line is lined up with this book. Charles is there in the place of his father, the Marrok. And of course, he brings his mate and Omega, Anna. Anna is very useful in situations like this and she proves that time and time again. <br><br>There is a lot going on with the story. Quite a few new characters, and some of the regulars. I like that, but at times it can feel a little overwhelming. I didn’t love that. And the fact that I listened may have made it a little more difficult to keep track of everything. I liked some of the new characters, but I did miss Asil from book one. I’m really hoping he’s in the next book. <br><br>There was some action and even some mystery, but what I loved most about this story was seeing the growth in Anna and Charles relationship. He’s learning the can’s and can’ts when it comes to his damaged wolf. Anna is able to open up more to Charles and trust him more. Not just her wolf doing this, but her as a person. It’s taken a lot of time for her to start to overcome her past and I love that she’s doing it and moving forward. <br> <br>I’m really enjoying this series. I can’t tell if I like it as much as the Mercy Thompson books- I really love those. With each and every book I’m liking it more and more. My husband tells me the next book is the best so far in the series so I’m sure I’ll be listening to it sooner rather than later! <br></span>
  <a data-text-id="3687415504966209750" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

Anna and Charles have just been enlisted to attend a summit to present Bran's controversial proposition: that the wolves should finally reveal themselves to humans. But the most feared Alpha in Europe is dead set against the plan--and it seems like someone else might be, too. When Anna is attacked by vampires using pack magic, the kind of power only werewolves should be able to draw on, Charles and Anna must combine their talents to hunt down whoever is behind it all--or risk losing everything ..."</i> - Page 4 of cover.<br /><br />تاریخ نخستین خوانش: روز دوازدهم ماه دسامبر سال 2016 میلادی<br /><br />عنوان: شکارگاه - کتاب 2 از محموعه آلفا و امگا؛ نویسنده: پاتریشیا بریگز؛ مترجم: آیدین کبیری؛ تهران، آذرباد، 1395؛ در 380ص؛ شابک دوره 9786006225579؛ شابک جلد یک 9786008537014؛ موضوع داستانهای خیال انگیز از نویسندگان امریکایی - سده 21م<br /><br />آنا لاتام نمی‌دانست زندگی تا چه حد می‌تواند پیچیده باشد، تا اینکه تبدیل به یک گرگینه شد. نمی‌دانست زندگی تا چه حد می‌تواند خطرناک باشد، تا اینکه با «چارلز کورنیک»، پسر «برن»، سردسته ی‌ گرگ‌ نماهای آمریکای شمالی جفت شد...؛ «آنا» و «چارلز» داوطلب شده ‌اند تا در نشست رهبران، پیشنهاد جنجالی «برن» را ارائه کنند، پیشنهادی که براساس آن، باید در نهایت، هویت اصلی‌ خویش را، برای انسان‌ها فاش کنند. اما رخدادها عملی‌ شدن پیشنهاد «برن» را دشوار می‌سازد. وقتی دسته ‌ای از خون ‌آشام‌ها با استفاده از جادویی که فقط گرگ‌نماها مجاز به استفاده از آن هستند، به «آنا» حمله می‌کنند؛ «چارلز» و «آنا»، باید استعدادها‌شان را روی هم بگذارند، و هرکسی را که پشت تمام این ماجراهاست پیدا کنند. در غیر این‌صورت همه چیز را از دست می‌دهند...؛ ا. شربیانی</span>

<div id="review_1954378617" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Tadiana ✩Night Owl☽" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Tadiana ✩Night Owl☽" href="/user/show/8734459-tadiana-night-owl">Tadiana ✩Night Owl☽</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/8734459-tadiana-night-owl?shelf=vampires-and-werewolves-oh-my">vampires-and-werewolves-oh-my</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/8734459-tadiana-night-owl?shelf=urban-fantasy">urban-fantasy</a>,

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1954378617" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer8117291401873379133">There's just something addictive about these books ... It just popped up in my Kindle last night and I opened it and the rest is history.<br/><br/><i>Hunting Ground</i> is a solid story in the ALPHA AND OMEGA series. Charles (an Alpha werewolf who acts as his father Bran's enforcer rather than being the head of a pack) and his mate Anna, an Omega werewolf, are sent on a mission to Seattle, to a meeting of Alpha werewolves from England, Spain, France and elsewhere. Bran is planning to go public with the fact that</span>
  <span id="freeText8117291401873379133" style="display:none">There's just something addictive about these books ... It just popped up in my Kindle last night and I opened it and the rest is history.<br /><br /><i>Hunting Ground</i> is a solid story in the ALPHA AND OMEGA series. Charles (an Alpha werewolf who acts as his father Bran's enforcer rather than being the head of a pack) and his mate Anna, an Omega werewolf, are sent on a mission to Seattle, to a meeting of Alpha werewolves from England, Spain, France and elsewhere. Bran is planning to go public with the fact that there are werewolves among humans; others strenuously oppose this move.<br /><br />Charles convinces Bran to let him represent Bran at this gathering, due to a premonition that Bran's going would result in his death. But now death is stalking Charles, Anna and others, and - other than the fact that a secretive and unusual gang of vampires is involved - no one knows who is behind the attacks and why. Meanwhile the werewolf meetings are going off the rails, primarily because of one French werewolf with a long and bloody history.<br /><br />Patricia Briggs slowly builds the tension in this story, intertwining the mystery with the development of her characters. Charles and Anna are still working out their relationship, and both are troubled by their respective pasts in different ways. It's a bit slow-paced, but still interesting, and with a great ending. The <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Beast_of_G%C3%A9vaudan" rel="nofollow noopener">Beast of Gévaudan</a> plays a key role. I love how Patricia Briggs pulls in monsters from actual folklore and weaves them into her plots!</span>
  <a data-text-id="8117291401873379133" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was ok"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was ok</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1846410428" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer15544477131969523556">💀 <b>Boring Outdated UF is Boring and Outdated Buddy Read</b> (BOUFiBaOBR™) with <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1825055319' rel='nofollow noopener'>Ashley</a> and <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/122412655' rel='nofollow noopener'>Angela</a> 💀<br/><br/><b><u>Actual rating</u>: 2.2 stars</b>. <i>Damn, I can be so generous sometimes, it's making me all teary-eyed and stuff.</i><br/><br/><b>This is such a delightful little series</b>. I loved <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/8141390-cry-wolf' rel='nofollow noopener'>book 1</a> so much that I just could NOT wait to read this instalment. And if someone tells you that this is total BS, that I <b>hated</b> book 1 and swore a <b>blood oath</b> to stay the fish away from this series for the rest of the entirety of my entire life, well that</span>
  <span id="freeText15544477131969523556" style="display:none">💀 <b>Boring Outdated UF is Boring and Outdated Buddy Read</b> (BOUFiBaOBR™) with <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1825055319" rel="nofollow noopener">Ashley</a> and <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/122412655" rel="nofollow noopener">Angela</a> 💀<br><br><b><u>Actual rating</u>: 2.2 stars</b>. <i>Damn, I can be so generous sometimes, it's making me all teary-eyed and stuff.</i><br><br><b>This is such a delightful little series</b>. I loved <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/8141390-cry-wolf" rel="nofollow noopener">book 1</a> so much that I just could NOT wait to read this instalment. And if someone tells you that this is total BS, that I <b>hated</b> book 1 and swore a <b>blood oath</b> to stay the fish away from this series for the rest of the entirety of my entire life, well that someone is completely full of <b>crappity crap</b>. The truthful truth is, I thought book 1 was nothing short of amazing, and was more looking forward to reading Hunting Ground than to having the <a href="http://bit.ly/2iHU8KE" rel="nofollow noopener">Scourge of Mexico</a> go all TACTILE on me. That should tell you something right there. And to be completely clear: no, the <b>Corruptor of Young Naïve Innocent Souls</b> (CoYNIS™) named Angela did NOT put a gun to my lovely little head to force me to read this book. Absolutely not. I did it of <b>my own free <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[if slightly masochistic <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> will</b>. Do you seriously think a nefarious breeder of murderous crustaceans such as I would let herself be <b>disgustingly manipulated</b> in such a despicable manner? Please don't be ridiculous, my Little Barnacles.<br><br><b>Soooooo</b>, after splendidly enrapturing me with Cry Wolf, Patricia Briggs positively enchanted me with this little book here. So much <b>captivating stuff</b> to be had in this instalment, I don't really know where to start. Will you give me a minute to think about it? <b>So lovely of you</b>, my Tiny Arthropods. Here, put some headphones on and listen to some soothing elevator music while I try and figure out how to do this.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1487262188i/21993113._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><i>What? You've never seen snailphones before? They're all the rage in my subaquatic kingdom! You really should go out more often, my Lovely Decapods.</i><br><br><b>Okay</b>, I'm ready to do the slightly vindictive thing now! Yay! You're welcome!<br><br>① <b>This book is a teensy little bit boring, flat, uninteresting and dull</b>. <br>But hey, it's not ALL bad, the book is lackluster, too. It kind of makes <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/421007.Nightlife__Cal_Leandros__1_" title="Nightlife (Cal Leandros #1) by Rob Thurman" rel="nofollow noopener">Nightlife</a> feel extremely exciting, actually. Which is <b>quite an achievement</b>, when you think about it, and means Hunting Ground here qualifies as a <b>Superiorly Efficient Cure for Insomnia</b> (SECfI™). See? Told you it was not ALL bad! There are some <b>fantastic, positive side effects</b> to reading this book! And you know what else? This is such an emotional flatland that the story comes with a <b>No Heart Attack Low Blood Pressure Guarantee</b> (NHLBPG™). Yep, that's just how exhilaratingly stimulating Hunting Ground is. Add to that the <b>fascinatingly fascinating</b> relationship crap that graces every single shrimping page of this wondrous little story, and you get one of the most <b>spellbinding experiences</b> ever. This really is <b>Gloriously Glorious Decaf Diet Non-Fat UF</b> (GGDDNFUF™) at its best! <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1461342216ra/18856498.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>② <b>This book is kinda sorta outdated</b>.<br>I do love vintage UF. Because it never makes you feel like you've read the story <b>hundreds of times</b>. Oh no, absolutely not. Good old tales about werewolf/vamp/silly fae/whatever wars are always <b>sooooo refreshing</b>. And quite original, too. And decidedly creative. What? You think I'm being a bit <b>too harsh</b> here? Because the book was written just 8 years ago? You couldn't be more wrong. Because <b>1/</b>I'm not like that, oh no, not me. I am <b>kindness and understanding</b> personified. Obviously. And because <b>2/</b>2009 in UF Wonderland equates to anciently ancient prehistory in Not-UF Wonderland. So there. Besides, I never said that this story being slightly outdated was a bad thing. Nope nope nope. To be honest, I think this <b>beautifully antiquated</b> touch gives the book a certain, irresistible je ne sais quoi. Which is <b>pretty scrumptious</b>, if you ask me. And partly explains why I loved the book <b>so shrimping much</b>. <br><br>③ <b>Our lovely female MC, Anna, is, you know, lovely and stuff</b>. <br>Some weird, twisted people like their heroines to be <b>ruthless, cunning, devious</b>, possibly <b>backstabbish</b>, slightly <b>cutthroatish</b> <s>bitches</s> chicks who slice slice slice cut cut cut their way through life. EW EW EW. Some people are <b>seriously disturbed</b>, if you ask me. I personally love my heroines to be <b>understanding, compassionate, peace-loving, soft-hearted, calming creatures</b> whose mission in life is to soothe and appease and tranquilize and stuff. Which is why I love Anna Dear soooooo much. I mean, not only does the girl sing Brahms lullabies, she also de-stresses the restless masses by playing <b>happy tunes from Sesame Street</b> on battered old pianos (don't ask). She very graciously plays along with darling grandpapas who sing Mr Bojangles in restaurants, too! How <b>delightfully delightful and overwhelmingly charming</b>! My Anna here is probably one of the mostest perfectest heroines ever: naturally talented, and a breathing, walking Xanax pill. A dream come true. <b>I think I'm in love</b>.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1487264401i/21993444.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br><b>You know</b>, I have done a lot of thinking about the average rating for this book. I mean, 4.26 stars? Seriously? I knew you Little Barnacles had <b>despicable book taste</b> and stuff, but this is taking it a bit too far. So I have come to the following indisputable conclusion: either you <s>raving lunatics</s> read it wrong <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[
  <i>so what else is new?</i>
 <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span>, I read it wrong <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[
  <i>hahaha, you can be so funny sometimes</i>
 <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> or I got my hunting grounds <b>all mixed up</b> and read <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/1289937.Stalking_Still_Hunting" rel="nofollow noopener">this</a> instead of Briggs' most glorious piece of UF <s>lethargy</s> excitement. <b>Yeah, that must be it</b>.<br><br>➽ And the moral of this <b>Bloody Shrimping Hell this Really is the Last Time I Read a Bloody Shrimping Book in this Bloody Shrimping Series Crappy Non Review</b> (BSHtRitLTIRaBSBitBSSCNR™) is: Angela, you made me read this thing. I love you. <b>You are SO dead</b>.<br> <br>✉ <i>Very private, confidential message to Patricia Briggs and her wondrously bilingual editorial team: next time you want to use "de nada" in a sentence, do your little selves a huge favor and ask a 5-year-old kid for help. I'm pretty sure that he/she will do a better job of it than you did in this book. You're welcome.</i><br> <br>· <b>Book 0.5</b>: <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1089504081" rel="nofollow noopener">Alpha &amp; Omega</a> ★★★★<br>· <b>Book 1</b>: <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1089501664" rel="nofollow noopener">Cry Wolf</a> ★★<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1479540926i/21203689._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>[Pre-review nonsense]<br><br><b>The good news is</b>, I did not hate it. <b>The bad news is</b>, I did not hate it. I mean, come on, a 2-star book that isn't rant-worthy? Who's ever heard of such a ridiculous thing?! <b>What a complete, total rip-off</b>! This is outrageous! This cannot be, Patricia Briggs! <b>This will not do</b>!<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1421684558i/13403936.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>►► Full <b>I Had Given Up on this Most Delightful Series but Ange is a Corruptor of Naïve Innocent Souls like Me So I Had no Choice but to Read this One Crappy Non Review</b> (IHGUotMDSbAiaCoNISlMSIHnCbtRtOCNR™) to come.</["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>

  <span id="freeText15490874398071097" style="display:none"><b> Audio book reread<br>Upgraded from 3 stars to 3.75 stars </b><br><br>I agree with everything I said the first time around, but I enjoyed this one much more the second time.<br>--------------------------------------<br><br><b> <i> “She was his and he hers.” </i> </b><br><br><a href="http://s177.photobucket.com/user/dawnygirl07/media/collagehuntingground.png.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1411978594i/11307165._SX540_.png" alt=" photo collagehuntingground.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><b> <i> “Women are the bloodthirsty sex. We get the reputation, but it is only because the women stand behind us, and say, 'Kill it. Squish it.” </i> </b><br><br>One month after they are mated and married, werewolves Anna and Charles must travel to Seattle to oversee a conference where the wolves discuss the issue of becoming open to the public. While they are there, hired vampire assassins begin attacking the Omega's, human and wolf.<br><br>This one took me a while to get through. I'm normally a huge Patricia Briggs fan, but for some reason this series isn't hitting it for me like the Mercy Thompson series did.<br><br><b> What I loved: </b><br><br>-Anna and Charles: I think the development of the relationship between these two characters is the only reason I will continue to read this series. Together and separately, Anna and Charles are some of the more interesting and unique characters I've read in a long time. But Briggs has a way of doing that.<br><br><b> <i> “I would slay dragons for you. I suspect that finding an unoccupied bedroom will be easier.” </i> </b><br><br>-The world-building: I am constantly wowed at the incredible job this author has done in creating this unique urban fantasy setting. Very few authors have done this for me. I want to go and visit! (Hopefully without becoming prey).<br><br>-The setting: It was Washington State, enough said. That place is awesome!<br><br><b> What didn't work: </b><br><br>-The pacing: OMG the pacing was so off with this book! It would go really slow, and then really fast, but then mostly slow and I had a hard time getting through this book.<br><br>-The constant reminders of pack hierarchy: We get it already, when dominant werewolves are around each other shit is about to go down. Stop using 50 pages to reiterate something that happened, but you can't tell at once because all of the wolves have to pull their dicks out and measure them. UGH.<br><br>So overall, I liked this book, but I didn't love it.<br><br><b> <i> “To make great art, you had to expose your soul, and some things should be left safely in the dark.” </i> </b><br><br><br>Lastly (and Gilmore Girls fans will understand) when they introduced a foreign wolf called Michel Girard, I immediately saw this:<br><a href="http://s177.photobucket.com/user/dawnygirl07/media/michel.png.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1411978594i/11307166.png" alt=" photo michel.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg">

<div id="review_1252084273" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1252084273" />
    <a title="♥Rachel♥" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/5481477-rachel"><img alt="♥Rachel♥" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1363996055p2/5481477.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1252084273?book_show_action=true">Apr 11, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="♥Rachel♥" class="user" itemprop="url" name="♥Rachel♥" href="/user/show/5481477-rachel">♥Rachel♥</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5481477-rachel?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5481477-rachel?shelf=audio-book">audio-book</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5481477-rachel?shelf=urban-fantasy">urban-fantasy</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5481477-rachel?shelf=mystery">mystery</a>
          </div>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1252084273" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer538247813469325687"><b>4.5 Stars<br/><br/>Re-read February 16th 2018. </b><br/><br/>Didn't leave much of a review the first time I read Hunting Ground (see below) so I'll add a bit more now.<br/><br/>Events pick up about four weeks after Cry Wolf, with Anna and Charles being sent off to Seattle for a conference/discussion about the Wolves coming out to the public. As Charles says, there are no negotiations, Bran has already decided that this will happen, because too many of the wrong people know of their existence and have used it as blackmail with th</span>
  <span id="freeText538247813469325687" style="display:none"><b>4.5 Stars<br /><br />Re-read February 16th 2018. </b><br /><br />Didn't leave much of a review the first time I read Hunting Ground (see below) so I'll add a bit more now.<br /><br />Events pick up about four weeks after Cry Wolf, with Anna and Charles being sent off to Seattle for a conference/discussion about the Wolves coming out to the public. As Charles says, there are no negotiations, Bran has already decided that this will happen, because too many of the wrong people know of their existence and have used it as blackmail with the wolves. When they come out, that can't happen anymore, and they can try and control how the world sees them. So this gathering of Packs from all over the world is a chance to hear concerns and for Bran, the Marrok, to offer aide to Packs who request it to ease the transition. <br /><br />Lots of posturing from other Alphas is expected and much attention is focused on Anna, being a rare Omega and the Mate of Charles. Charles' reputation as the ruthless enforcer of his father, the Marrok, makes him taking a Mate all the more interesting. But they encounter more than just harmless curiosity. Vampires attack Anna, using what appears to be Pack magic, and they have to wonder is this a plot to foil Bran's plan to reveal the Wolves existence or is there more going on here? <br /><br />I LOVE this series so much! Anna and Charles go through some bumpy times early in their relationship, since their wolf-half decided their mating before they really got to know each other. Each have insecurities and vulnerabilities, and sometimes because they don't want to look like a needy fool to the other so they kept their concerns to themselves causing some unnecessary misinterpretations. They make progress, bit by bit, making my heart melt for them a little more with every chapter. They are so very in love, and their new relationship will take some time to sort out, but that's okay, because they have time. Lots of time! <br /><br />I love that Anna is gaining more confidence and ends up being a fierce protector of Charles in many ways. Charles understands some of Anna's insecurities, thanks to the brutalization she suffered at the hands of her previous Pack, and he's so protective and supportive of her overcoming her fears and replenishing her self-confidence. What she accomplishes in this installment really shows Anna's an intelligent, powerful, instinctively protective force. <br /><br />Holter Graham is an excellent narrator! He brings both Anna and Charles to life. I've already starting listening to the next installment.<br /><br />Review first time through:<br /><b><br />I'm loving Charles and Anna a little more with each book.</b></span>
  <a data-text-id="538247813469325687" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_1100867859" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1100867859" />
    <a title="Alex is The Romance Fox" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/6663962-alex-is-the-romance-fox"><img alt="Alex is The Romance Fox" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1428866380p2/6663962.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1100867859?book_show_action=true">Nov 08, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Alex is The Romance Fox" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Alex is The Romance Fox" href="/user/show/6663962-alex-is-the-romance-fox">Alex is The Romance Fox</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="ebook 9781101133484" href="/book/show/8922438-hunting-ground">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6663962-alex-is-the-romance-fox?shelf=vampire-shapeshifters">vampire-shapeshifters</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6663962-alex-is-the-romance-fox?shelf=authors-a-h">authors-a-h</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6663962-alex-is-the-romance-fox?shelf=urban-fantasy">urban-fantasy</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6663962-alex-is-the-romance-fox?shelf=romance">romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6663962-alex-is-the-romance-fox?shelf=lendable">lendable</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6663962-alex-is-the-romance-fox?shelf=series">series</a>
          </div>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1100867859" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer4599500013824002593">Hunting Ground continues with Charles and Anna, newly mated and working on their relationship.<blockquote>
  
    <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1437836372i/15634090.jpg' alt=' photo download_zpsahn7ckee.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
  
</blockquote> They are sent by the Marok to attend a meeting in Seattle with werewolves around the world. Bran, the Marok and Charles father has decided to publicly announce to the world the existence of wolves. The gathering is to discuss the idea and persuade the packs that this is a good idea.<br/><br/>I love seeing this mystical and magical world that the author has created evolving with the introduction of ne</span>
  <span id="freeText4599500013824002593" style="display:none">Hunting Ground continues with Charles and Anna, newly mated and working on their relationship.<blockquote>
  
    <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1437836372i/15634090.jpg" alt=" photo download_zpsahn7ckee.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
  
</blockquote> They are sent by the Marok to attend a meeting in Seattle with werewolves around the world. Bran, the Marok and Charles father has decided to publicly announce to the world the existence of wolves. The gathering is to discuss the idea and persuade the packs that this is a good idea.<br><br>I love seeing this mystical and magical world that the author has created evolving with the introduction of new and interesting and total believable characters…the wolf packs from countries outside America and their dynamics and of course we get to see the regulars as well.<br><br>This is a fast paced, action paced story filled with some unexpected twists and revelations – I was certainly kept guessing!!!!!!<br>It’s lovely to see Anna coming into her own and her developing relationship with Charles’s pack. Their bond is amazing and beautiful to see…<blockquote>
  
    <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1437836372i/15634091.jpg" alt=" photo download204_zpsjo1eound.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
  
</blockquote> And it’s lovely to see how they bring something good to each other……<blockquote>
  
    <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1437836372i/15634092.jpg" alt=" photo snow20cold20fantasy20art20artwork20wolves201280x85320wallpaper_www.animalhi.com_20_zpsypcmwedm.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
  
</blockquote> This is turning out to be a series as good as the Mercy Thompson one. Can’t wait to read the next installment!!</span>

<div id="review_66731347" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/66731347" />
    <a title="Mel" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/2295424-mel"><img alt="Mel" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1305638929p2/2295424.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/66731347?book_show_action=true">Aug 09, 2009</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Mel" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Mel" href="/user/show/2295424-mel">Mel</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2295424-mel?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2295424-mel?shelf=pnr">pnr</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer66731347" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer10550437170193567532">First I'd like to comment that the description on Goodreads is not a good description of the contents of the book (you'll see what I mean after you've read it) and does not match the description on the book jacket, which is a much better summary:<br/><i>“Anna Latham didn’t know how complicated life could be until she became a werewolf. And until she was mated to Charles Cornick, the son- and enforcer- of Bran, the leader of the North American werewolves, she didn’t know how dangerous it could be either.</i></span>
  <span id="freeText10550437170193567532" style="display:none">First I'd like to comment that the description on Goodreads is not a good description of the contents of the book (you'll see what I mean after you've read it) and does not match the description on the book jacket, which is a much better summary:<br /><i>“Anna Latham didn’t know how complicated life could be until she became a werewolf. And until she was mated to Charles Cornick, the son- and enforcer- of Bran, the leader of the North American werewolves, she didn’t know how dangerous it could be either. <br />Anna and Charles have just been enlisted to attend a summit to present Bran’s controversial proposition: that the wolves should finally reveal themselves to humans. But the most feared Alpha in Europe is dead set against the plan- and it seems like someone else might be too. When Anna is attacked by vampires using pack magic, the kind of power only werewolves should be able to draw on, Charles and Anna must combine their talents to hunt down whoever is behind it all- or risk losing everything. “</i><br /><br />I read <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/2355575.Cry_Wolf__Alpha___Omega___1_" title="Cry Wolf (Alpha &amp; Omega, #1) by Patricia Briggs" rel="nofollow noopener">Cry Wolf</a> (the first book in the Alpha &amp; Omega series) a couple of days ago and rated it three stars (which still seems a bit too harsh but 3,5 isn’t available; I need to start a petition or something). <br />Cry Wolf was a decent read. Plotwise I wasn’t so in love with the action because it was too simple and too much based on a string of coincidences. But what I loved about the book was the romance, which pretty much centered around Anna and Charles getting to know each other and learning to trust each other, after their wolves had decided to mate. <br /><br />In <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/5292853.Hunting_Ground__Alpha___Omega___2_" title="Hunting Ground (Alpha &amp; Omega, #2) by Patricia Briggs" rel="nofollow noopener">Hunting Ground</a> we’re a month later in time. Charles and Anna are now married as also their human sides have accepted to be mated. Their mating bond though, still has to be developed and this depends on both Anna’s ability to fully trust Charles as well as Charles’ ability to open himself up to her. <br /><br />The deepening of their relationship is an ongoing process in the book and is beautifully worked out. Like last time, we get to be in both Anna’s and Charles’ heads and experience their doubts, fears and deep need for one another. <br />I love Anna and Charles together and I especially like reading Charles’ point of view about it. <br />Being his father’s assassin has made Charles block out deep feelings and emotions and he’s often overwhelmed by Anna. She in her turn doesn’t always know how to deal with Charles, who she (rightfully I think) calls a force of nature. Their ability to see one another for what they truly are, is the strength in their relationship. <br /><br />The way Briggs describes the mating bond -the intimacy of knowing and feeling what your mate is going through- is so great it almost makes you sad that us humans aren’t capable of such a thing on such a level. Which is a great accomplishment by Briggs considering the fact that she absolutely does not glorify the supernatural creatures she writes about. Quite the opposite: I sure wouldn’t want to be a werewolf. (Well... maybe if they add a Charles to the package I’d consider…)<br /><br />Unlike Cry Wolf, I wasn’t put off by the action plot this time. There were a few minor things though I wasn’t too happy with. <br />First: Charles is supposed to be his father’s enforcer for over a 150 years and is supposedly ‘very very good at his job’ as it keeps getting mentioned. But suddenly it seems like Anna is the key figure in everything he does, and it makes you wonder how he was able to pull off the job all by himself so very smoothly the 149 years before. <br />Second: the villain to me was clear from the beginning. This is the third book of Briggs that I’ve read so far and till now she keeps using the same ways to introduce certain characters. It's soon clear which characters are ‘bad’ and which are there to distract the attention.<br />Still, the plot was very entertaining and nicely worked out. <br /><br />So again, a very decent read by Patricia Briggs. Will round it up to a full 4 stars this time. I’m anxiously awaiting the third novel. <br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="10550437170193567532" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_47832070" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/47832070" />
    <a title=" Danielle The Book Huntress (Back to the Books)" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/1570669-danielle-the-book-huntress-back-to-the-books"><img alt=" Danielle The Book Huntress (Back to the Books)" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1403239075p2/1570669.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/47832070?book_show_action=true">Feb 28, 2009</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title=" Danielle The Book Huntress (Back to the Books)" class="user" itemprop="url" name=" Danielle The Book Huntress (Back to the Books)" href="/user/show/1570669-danielle-the-book-huntress-back-to-the-books"> Danielle The Book Huntress (Back to the Books)</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>


          <div><span class="uitext greyText">Recommends it for: </span>
           <span class="uitext reviewText">Urban fantasy readers</span></div>

        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1570669-danielle-the-book-huntress-back-to-the-books?shelf=part-of-a-series">part-of-a-series</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1570669-danielle-the-book-huntress-back-to-the-books?shelf=werewolf">werewolf</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1570669-danielle-the-book-huntress-back-to-the-books?shelf=heroine-i-adore">heroine-i-adore</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1570669-danielle-the-book-huntress-back-to-the-books?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1570669-danielle-the-book-huntress-back-to-the-books?shelf=dangerous-hero-2012-general-reading">dangerous-hero-2012-general-reading</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1570669-danielle-the-book-huntress-back-to-the-books?shelf=supercouple">supercouple</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1570669-danielle-the-book-huntress-back-to-the-books?shelf=scary-sexy-cool-dangerous-hero">scary-sexy-cool-dangerous-hero</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1570669-danielle-the-book-huntress-back-to-the-books?shelf=fated-to-be-mated">fated-to-be-mated</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1570669-danielle-the-book-huntress-back-to-the-books?shelf=desert-island-keepers">desert-island-keepers</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1570669-danielle-the-book-huntress-back-to-the-books?shelf=famous-literary-historical-characte">famous-literary-historical-characte</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer47832070" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer9120450995516876877">I am glad I took my time reading this. I think there are so many levels to this novel that I could miss if I breezed through. I like how simple Briggs writes. Not a lot of nonsense, extraneous prose that bogs down the story. Despite her concise narrative, she conveys so much, filling the novel with an emotional power. Her characters have a distinct feel to them from other writers. I like that she puts their flaws out there unashamedly, and it makes you love the characters even more. <br/><br/>I will freel</span>
  <span id="freeText9120450995516876877" style="display:none">I am glad I took my time reading this. I think there are so many levels to this novel that I could miss if I breezed through. I like how simple Briggs writes. Not a lot of nonsense, extraneous prose that bogs down the story. Despite her concise narrative, she conveys so much, filling the novel with an emotional power. Her characters have a distinct feel to them from other writers. I like that she puts their flaws out there unashamedly, and it makes you love the characters even more. <br /><br />I will freely admit I like the scary hero that everyone fears, but the one woman who looked into his heart and feels safe with him, and is not afraid to love him. I think that Anna and Charles have that sort of bond that is symbiotic. It doesn't really apply to call it yin and yang, but there are elements of softness and strength coming together. Truly though, their strengths complement each other. And they aren't trying to modify each other to make a more comfortable fit for the other. It's more a matter of growing in their knowledge of each other, and growing together. I find their relationship very fascinating and fulfilling, and that's another reason why I read this book slowly.<br /><br /><br />The storyline was very good as well. A lot of intrigue here, to see who was trying to destroy the Marrok's plan for an alliance when the werewolves reveal themselves to the world. The suspense was done cleverly, because you look at the key players, think someone looks likely, but look away to focus on someone else, and then you realize that things aren't the way they seem. I liked how she kept me guessing.<br /><br />The werewolf parts are fantastic as usual. Just utterly fascinating. Another thing to appreciate from all angles as I read. And throw some faerie and King Arthur stuff in there, and I start thinking this story is tailor made for me. This is my kind of urban fantasy. Naturalistic characters with identifiable motivations, enough grit to keep my heart beating fast, a heroine whose strength comes from within, and who grows right in front of my eyes, for Anna is a phoenix who rose from the ashes. A to-die-for hero who makes me sigh even as he makes others shudder with fear. But then you see his soft spot is his Anna. How can I resist that? Just the right dose of romance that fits into the story so well, it neither distracts or detracts from the fantasy elements. Everything my heart desires, except the book was over, and I still wanted more.<br /><br />I love you, Patricia Briggs.</span>
  <a data-text-id="9120450995516876877" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

<div id="review_2381544253" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2381544253" />
    <a title="Paula" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/16174645-paula"><img alt="Paula" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1605390346p2/16174645.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2381544253?book_show_action=true">Apr 30, 2020</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Paula" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Paula" href="/user/show/16174645-paula">Paula</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>


          <div><span class="uitext greyText">Recommends it for: </span>
           <span class="uitext reviewText">Werewolf + vampire fans</span></div>

        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/16174645-paula?shelf=favorite-authors">favorite-authors</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/16174645-paula?shelf=series">series</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/16174645-paula?shelf=romance">romance</a>,

          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2381544253" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer7031311848827218149">Fantastic...my favorite guilty pleasure...<br/><br/>Briggs has two series out that I both adore. The first is the Mercy Thompson series which I have been reading with my son for years. The Alpha + Omega series is a prequel and very well done. I am such a big fan of both.<br/><br/>Such marvelous escapism. Do read if you like werewolves with a bit of romance thrown in.<br/><br/>5 out of 5 stars</span>

<div id="review_909399106" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/909399106" />
    <a title="Carmel (Rabid Reads)" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/4561998-carmel-rabid-reads"><img alt="Carmel (Rabid Reads)" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1396922701p2/4561998.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/909399106?book_show_action=true">Apr 13, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Carmel (Rabid Reads)" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Carmel (Rabid Reads)" href="/user/show/4561998-carmel-rabid-reads">Carmel (Rabid Reads)</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Audiobook 9781440644634" href="/book/show/9816086-hunting-ground">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4561998-carmel-rabid-reads?shelf=werewolves">werewolves</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4561998-carmel-rabid-reads?shelf=audio">audio</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4561998-carmel-rabid-reads?shelf=audio-2014">audio-2014</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer909399106" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer15520575671699483935"><b>Reviewed by: <a href='http://rabidreads.ca/2015/02/audiobook-review-hunting-ground-by-patricia-briggs.html' rel='nofollow noopener'>Rabid Reads</a>.</b><br/><br/>HUNTING GROUND had a lot of interesting morsels in it from both a mythology and a story standpoint; readers get to learn about fae, vampires and dragons (!!!), witness firsthand how Bran’s decision to bring the werewolves out to the public came to be, and observe the continuing evolution of Anna & Charles’ relationship. No author does light/dark quite like Patricia Briggs, and this audiobook really emblazoned that fact by putting these preternaturals’ best and worst qual</span>
  <span id="freeText15520575671699483935" style="display:none"><b>Reviewed by: <a href="http://rabidreads.ca/2015/02/audiobook-review-hunting-ground-by-patricia-briggs.html" rel="nofollow noopener">Rabid Reads</a>.</b><br /><br />HUNTING GROUND had a lot of interesting morsels in it from both a mythology and a story standpoint; readers get to learn about fae, vampires and dragons (!!!), witness firsthand how Bran’s decision to bring the werewolves out to the public came to be, and observe the continuing evolution of Anna &amp; Charles’ relationship. No author does light/dark quite like Patricia Briggs, and this audiobook really emblazoned that fact by putting these preternaturals’ best and worst qualities on display. Holter Graham’s narration continues to leave me in thrall, and the murder mystery plot line made hours of listening time feel like mere minutes. Now I understand why this series trumps MERCY THOMPSON for many.<br /><br />I enjoyed being a fly on the wall at the werewolf conference; pack dynamics have always fascinated me, and the political aspects that Briggs brought to the fore were so well executed that it was impossible not to get caught-up in the discussions. This novel really showcased the best and worst of shifter society from The Beast who likes to feast on human flesh, to Arthur who obviously wasn’t playing with a full deck of cards, to Anna who’s slowly coming back from the dead. I hadn’t expected to meet another Omega already what with them being extremely rare and all, but it seems like Ric was as clueless about his nature as Latham, so it was amusing watching them attempt to fill-in the blanks together.<br /><br />In spite of all of the mad goings-on in this tale, Anna &amp; Charles still remain the driving force behind this series. I love how flawed their characters are, and how they continually adapt to each other in an effort to strengthen their mate bond. The open communication that exists between them is a breath of fresh air when compared to other couples in this genre where relationship drama has become the norm. I liked how the author added a historical element to HUNTING GROUND by putting her own werewolf spin on King Arthur, although I do wish that Latham hadn’t been coveted by yet another certifiable shifter so soon after leaving her first pack. Her kill count is staggeringly high after only two installments.<br /><br />Holter Graham’s narration made an impression on me in CRY WOLF, and in this audio he went above and beyond his original performance. He demonstrated great flexibility and flair by bringing the foreign wolves to life with various accents while still staying true to the original voices of Anna &amp; Charles, although the latter was admittedly somewhat modified. His delivery was both emotionally poignant and intense which were contributing factors to this story’s believably and further increased the purity of the characters. Graham’s inflections made the changes in POVs obvious, and I can’t wait to see what he does with FAIR GAME.<br /><br />HUNTING GROUND should be on every audiobook listener’s playlist.</span>
  <a data-text-id="15520575671699483935" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

    <div class="section">
      

<div id="review_870064061" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/870064061" />
    <a title="Angela" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/4255477-angela"><img alt="Angela" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1398251387p2/4255477.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/870064061?book_show_action=true">Mar 02, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Angela" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Angela" href="/user/show/4255477-angela">Angela</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/8130498-hunting-ground">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4255477-angela?shelf=urban-fantasy">urban-fantasy</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4255477-angela?shelf=kindle">kindle</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4255477-angela?shelf=2015-read">2015-read</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4255477-angela?shelf=2014-read">2014-read</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4255477-angela?shelf=2017-read">2017-read</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4255477-angela?shelf=2018-read">2018-read</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4255477-angela?shelf=poc">poc</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer870064061" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer4783809856372677678">January 2018 Re-read. Buddy read with Sarah<br/>January 2017 Re-read: Buddy read with Sarah<br/>December 2015 re-read: Buddy read with <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1472923875' rel='nofollow noopener'>Sarah</a><br/><br/>This is such a romantic story. Charles and Anna are still really new in their relationship here, so we get a lot of time with them figuring it out. And unlike a lot of romantic stories - it's not all figured out between the sheets. Sex is an important part of (any) relationship, and definitely one thing that they're figuring out here, but it's not the only thing - the</span>
  <span id="freeText4783809856372677678" style="display:none">January 2018 Re-read. Buddy read with Sarah<br />January 2017 Re-read: Buddy read with Sarah<br />December 2015 re-read: Buddy read with <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1472923875" rel="nofollow noopener">Sarah</a><br /><br />This is such a romantic story. Charles and Anna are still really new in their relationship here, so we get a lot of time with them figuring it out. And unlike a lot of romantic stories - it's not all figured out between the sheets. Sex is an important part of (any) relationship, and definitely one thing that they're figuring out here, but it's not the only thing - they talk, and they get to know each other a lot better in this novel. I appreciate all the time we spend with both of them as they become even closer. And seeing Anna grow and become even more comfortable in her skin is incredibly satisfying.<br /><br />The plot moves quickly, and is just the right amount of intricate. I liked all the further information we get as a result of what Charles and Anna are up to, and involved in. It's also unexpectedly funny. Much like Charles. I love how no one expects him to have a sense of humor, and he works to keep it that way, but he's constantly kidding and joking with and for Anna. <br /><br />Next we go back to Mercy's POV, in <i>Blood Bound</i>. I'm loving this series re-read.<br /><br /><br /><br />Previous review:<br />Of the first three stories (Alpha &amp; Omega, Cry Wolf, and Hunting Ground) this is definitely the most romantic. The pacing of the story is tight and moves along quickly, and we really get a chance to delve into the politics of the werewolves - around the world. At the same time we get to know Charles and Anna even better, and watch their relationship grow, which is my favorite part.<br /><br />Anna still has some issues with the abuse she suffered at the hands of her old pack. I love how Patricia Briggs handles this, it's not a constant fear, but it comes through at random moments and overwhelms her. She struggles against it, and talks herself past it frequently, but that's not always possible. It's shown beautifully at the beginning, Charles is drawing deeper and deeper into himself and his frustrations, and Anna has plans to bring him out of it by ambush. There's still that ingrained moment of hesitation about making him mad, what a much larger, more dominant wolf could do to her. Logically she knows he would never hurt her, and she knows that in her heart too, but it's hard to overcome what years of abuse will drill into a person. Even worried about that, Anna does it anyway - because she loves Charles.<br /><br />Seeing their relationship grow, and deepen, is a true joy. The comfort, and easiness between them continues to grow. That she can tease him, tickle him, and have fun with him shows just how far Anna's come. That Charles plays with her, shares private jokes, and can generally be a "lovebird" is perfect. <br /><br />I also really love how they're both adjusting to each other. They talk about it at one point and Anna asks if Charles is as confused as she is, and he says that he's not, but that he's differently confused because he'd had so long to settle into himself and being alone that the transition is different for him. Charles isn't a big talker, doesn't always trust his words to be what he wants them to be, but I love that he makes a real effort for Anna when she needs it.<br /><br />The mystery part of it is interesting, though I don't think it's hard to figure out who the ultimate "bad-guy" is - I can't recall if I did my first time reading it.<br /><br /><br />I think I'll just add some favorite quotes here, nothing too spoilery, but be warned if you don't like to read anything like that :)<br /><br /><blockquote>She gave him a happy look as he followed her out on the water-soaked wooden walk. "This could be fun," she said, then turned, took a running step, and did a couple of back flips - like a middle-school kid at recess. He stopped where he was, lust and love and fear rising up in a surge of emotion he did not, for all his years, have any idea how to deal with.<br /><br />"What?" she asked, a little breathless from her gymnastics. She brushed her wavy heair out of her face and gave him a serious look. "Is there something wrong?"<br /><br />He could hardly tell her that he was afraid because he didn't know what he'd do if something happened to her. That his sudden, unexpected reaction had brought Brother Wolf to the fore. She threw his balance off; his control - which had become almost effortless over the years - was erratic at best.</blockquote><br /><br />***<br /><br /><blockquote>"You are a remarkable man, Charles Cornick." <br /><br />He wrapped his arms around her shoulders and put his chin on the top of her head. "I know," he confided lightly. "And often under-appreciated by those who don't know any better."<br /><br />She poked him with a finger and looked up at him. "And funny - though I expect that is another facet of your character that goes unappreciated even more often than your remarkableness."<br /><br />"Some people don't even notice," he said in a mock-mournful voice.</blockquote><br /><br />***<br /><br /><blockquote>"Do you remember when I told you that you were my mate - and you responded by telling me you didn't like sex?"<br /><br />She giggled at his smug tone. "I thought it only fair to warn you."</blockquote><br /><br />***<br /><br /><blockquote>She was on the far side, leaving two cold feet of mattress between them. He knew that she'd fall asleep like that...and then gradually move over until she was plastered against him. Then he could go to sleep, too.</blockquote><br /><br />***<br /><br /><blockquote>"...I love your touch. Touch me anytime. Any place. Anywhere." It was heartfelt, and honest... &lt;&lt;*snip*&gt;&gt; "Pet me," he told her. "I like it."</blockquote></span>
  <a data-text-id="4783809856372677678" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

<div id="review_49583611" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/49583611" />
    <a title="MelissaB" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/1320046-melissab"><img alt="MelissaB" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1245899832p2/1320046.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/49583611?book_show_action=true">Mar 17, 2009</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="MelissaB" class="user" itemprop="url" name="MelissaB" href="/user/show/1320046-melissab">MelissaB</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>


          <div><span class="uitext greyText">Recommends it for: </span>
           <span class="uitext reviewText">werewolf romance fans who like a little mystery in their books</span></div>

        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1320046-melissab?shelf=2014-reads">2014-reads</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1320046-melissab?shelf=audio-book-i-own">audio-book-i-own</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1320046-melissab?shelf=2009-reads">2009-reads</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1320046-melissab?shelf=paranormal-romance">paranormal-romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1320046-melissab?shelf=2017-reads">2017-reads</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1320046-melissab?shelf=abused-heroine">abused-heroine</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1320046-melissab?shelf=werewolves">werewolves</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1320046-melissab?shelf=alpha-and-omega-series">alpha-and-omega-series</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer49583611" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer18146800669874115565">Hunting Ground is the third entry into the Alpha and Omega series. The first story was "Alpha and Omega" in the On the Prowl anthology and the second was a stand alone book, Cry Wolf. The series follows Anna and Charles after they meet in the first book and find out they are mates, then they must work their way through learning to accept the mating bond and work out their life together.<br/><br/>Anna was abused by her first pack which features heavily in the story as she tries to overcome her emotional sc</span>
  <span id="freeText18146800669874115565" style="display:none">Hunting Ground is the third entry into the Alpha and Omega series. The first story was "Alpha and Omega" in the On the Prowl anthology and the second was a stand alone book, Cry Wolf. The series follows Anna and Charles after they meet in the first book and find out they are mates, then they must work their way through learning to accept the mating bond and work out their life together.<br /><br />Anna was abused by her first pack which features heavily in the story as she tries to overcome her emotional scars. She is an Omega wolf, which means that she makes the pack feel happy and is outside the typical pack structure. She struggles with figuring out exactly where she stands in the pack because she was told she was the most submissive in the pack by her abusive former pack, which is not true at all but she needs to refind her strength. <br /><br />Charles is the son of Bran, The Marrok aka leader of all the wolves. By necessity, Charles has become his father's killer for wolves who break pack law. Charles keeps himself separate from all the wolves because he knows it will be easier to execute casual acquaintances than close friends. He doesn't quite know what to do with Anna because he loves her but has trouble opening himself up totally to the mating bond because he is afraid Anna will see him as a killer and not be able to love him. Charles knows that Anna is still afraid of him sometimes, especially in bed because of the abuse she suffered. He does everything he can to help her heal, he even allows her more freedom when she needs it because he knows she needs to stand on her own despite his wolf's need to keep her as safe as possible. They both love each other and are slowly opening up enough to show it.<br /><br />In this story, Charles and Anna travel to Seattle to meet with wolves from all over the world to discuss terms for the unveiling of wolves to the human population. Bran was supposed to go but Charles argued with him until he let Charles go in his place. Charles's grandfather was a Native American shaman and his father is witch-born, so he sees things that most people don't and the spirits told him that his father could die if he went to Seattle. So Charles and Anna go in his place to relay The Marrok's terms to the wolf alphas. <br /><br />Once in Seattle, Charles and Anna meet up with the local wolf pack and Dana, a Fae who is helping keep the peace with the wolves for a price. Soon after the negotiations begin, Anna is attacked and almost kidnapped by vampires. Before they have a chance to investigate, murders start to occur and more attacks come. Charles and Anna need to determine who is behind the attacks before they end up dead or the talks are ruined.<br /><br />I really enjoyed this book, Anna and Charles are great main characters who grow and learn more about each other with each book. I love seeing Anna regain her strength and courage. Charles is a great hero who has a lot of compassion and love for Anna but sees himself as a cold-blooded killer. Poor guy! The mystery in Patricia Briggs books is always very interesting. Her mythology of wolves who are very complex, vampires who are pretty vicious and the Fae who can be downright scary make up a very interesting world. I am really enjoying this story and learning more about Bran and Charles who we originally meet in the Mercy Thompson series. I think Patricia Briggs is a very talented author, I recommend checking out this series and the Mercy Thompson series which I love because the heroine is wonderful. I think the Alpha and Omega series is a very good werewolf series that has a romance and mystery.</span>
  <a data-text-id="18146800669874115565" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

  <span id="freeText16122995964852396124" style="display:none">4.5 stars.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1526225621ra/25533405.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I like the slow built of their relationship. Not sudden nor perfect, tripping and stumbling along the way trying to find the right step and balance to their relationship.<br>Anna turned Charles’s world up side down, and he doesn’t know how to cope with everything that he feels for her. He somehow locked away his human side with feelings, so he can be the hitman his father wants.<br>Now, Anna is his world and nothing is more important than her safety. He sucks at communication and many times they both fail at explanations, but there is trust and love, and a bond that no one can break. But that doesn’t mean their relationship is perfect, but you can see that they are trying.<br><br><i>
  <b>"I keep feeling like we're doing it wrong," she said. "That this bond between us is meant to be much more than we're allowing it to be."<br>"There is no wrong between us," he told her.</b>
</i><br><br>Charles doesn’t just love her, he treasures her.<br><br><br>Anna was abused and she’s traumatised but that doesn’t make her weak, just afraid. But when she needs to, she faces down her fears and becomes stronger. I have a feeling that in time she will overcome her fears and become even stronger, like Charles said, <i>Rome wasn’t built in a day</i> and I can’t wait to see who Anna becomes.<br><br><i>
  <b>It had felt good to defend herself against Chastel, even if it was only with words. She was tired of being afraid of her own shadow-and for a little while she hadn't been afraid at all. She liked it.</b>
</i><br><br>Charles doesn’t enforce his straight upon her so he can protect and feel good about it. Many times he wants to hide her somewhere away so she can be safe, but he knows that’s not right.<br><br><i>
  <b>"If it would benefit you, I would kill every wolf here. But there are things that you need to do - and interfering with that is not protecting, not in my book. The best way for me to protect you is to encourage you to be able to protect yourself."</b>
</i><br><br>Love it!</span>
