<div id="review_341275629" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/341275629" />
    <a title="Suzanne (Under the Covers Book blog)" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/3575839-suzanne-under-the-covers-book-blog"><img alt="Suzanne (Under the Covers Book blog)" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1583236251p2/3575839.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/341275629?book_show_action=true">Jun 02, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Suzanne (Under the Covers Book blog)" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Suzanne (Under the Covers Book blog)" href="/user/show/3575839-suzanne-under-the-covers-book-blog">Suzanne (Under the Covers Book blog)</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/8130498-hunting-ground">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3575839-suzanne-under-the-covers-book-blog?shelf=genre-urban-fantasy">genre-urban-fantasy</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3575839-suzanne-under-the-covers-book-blog?shelf=hero-mad-bad-and-dangerous-to-know">hero-mad-bad-and-dangerous-to-know</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3575839-suzanne-under-the-covers-book-blog?shelf=va-va-voom-vampires">va-va-voom-vampires</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3575839-suzanne-under-the-covers-book-blog?shelf=shifters">shifters</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3575839-suzanne-under-the-covers-book-blog?shelf=best-of-the-best-2012">best-of-the-best-2012</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3575839-suzanne-under-the-covers-book-blog?shelf=hero-i-wanna-hug">hero-i-wanna-hug</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3575839-suzanne-under-the-covers-book-blog?shelf=hero-hot-male-in-my-harem">hero-hot-male-in-my-harem</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3575839-suzanne-under-the-covers-book-blog?shelf=faves-kings-of-the-harem">faves-kings-of-the-harem</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3575839-suzanne-under-the-covers-book-blog?shelf=mages-witches-magic-users">mages-witches-magic-users</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3575839-suzanne-under-the-covers-book-blog?shelf=genre-mystery">genre-mystery</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer341275629" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer15209242471504862852">Patricia Briggs has once again ensnared me, I LOVED this book! <br/><br/><i>Huntung Ground</i> is set just before the werewolves come out to the public and Charles and Anna go to a meeting with all the European werewolves to soothe some fears...not that it works out that way of course. I thought it was a little better then <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/2355575.Cry_Wolf__Alpha___Omega___1_' title='Cry Wolf (Alpha & Omega, #1) by Patricia Briggs' rel='nofollow noopener'>Cry Wolf</a>, mainly because I found the story a bit more interesting there was more to get into as it was slightly more complex. <br/><br/>It also shows Charles and Anna's developing relationship. Part of </span>
  <span id="freeText15209242471504862852" style="display:none">Patricia Briggs has once again ensnared me, I LOVED this book! <br /><br /><i>Huntung Ground</i> is set just before the werewolves come out to the public and Charles and Anna go to a meeting with all the European werewolves to soothe some fears...not that it works out that way of course. I thought it was a little better then <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/2355575.Cry_Wolf__Alpha___Omega___1_" title="Cry Wolf (Alpha &amp; Omega, #1) by Patricia Briggs" rel="nofollow noopener">Cry Wolf</a>, mainly because I found the story a bit more interesting there was more to get into as it was slightly more complex. <br /><br />It also shows Charles and Anna's developing relationship. Part of what I like about this series is that the relationships are more real, Anna has been through 3 years of trauma an just because she has found a mate doesn't mean her psyche is immediately fixed and she is shiny and new again. I like that she is still wary as it seems more realistic but it also gives you an idea of how tough she is. As for Charles *dreamy sigh* I am sooo in love with Charles it is always the silent and deadly ones that get to me!<br /><br />Oh and Moira (the blind witch) and Tom from one of the PB's novella's are in this as well!</span>
  <a data-text-id="15209242471504862852" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_1620238678" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1620238678" />
    <a title="Wanda" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/9246169-wanda"><img alt="Wanda" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1528903039p2/9246169.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1620238678?book_show_action=true">Apr 25, 2016</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Wanda" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Wanda" href="/user/show/9246169-wanda">Wanda</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/9246169-wanda?shelf=urban-fantasy">urban-fantasy</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/9246169-wanda?shelf=werewolves-shifters">werewolves-shifters</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/9246169-wanda?shelf=favourites">favourites</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/9246169-wanda?shelf=fantasy">fantasy</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/9246169-wanda?shelf=female-authors">female-authors</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/9246169-wanda?shelf=read-in-2020">read-in-2020</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/9246169-wanda?shelf=fae-fairy">fae-fairy</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/9246169-wanda?shelf=used-books">used-books</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/9246169-wanda?shelf=read-in-2016">read-in-2016</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/9246169-wanda?shelf=vampires">vampires</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1620238678" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer14005879102837894290"><b>2020 Re-read </b><br/><br/>Urban fantasy is such a great pleasure! I love these tales of werewolves, vampires, fae, and witches, all located in contemporary cities. I'm particularly partial to stories of the fae and vampires. They make such great main characters or wonderful villains. This story gives us both of my favourites as the bad guys, making Charles and Anna work hard to keep this summit meeting on an even keel.<br/><br/>Anna gets to show her resilience more than once. Everyone thinks she is a weak creature, bu</span>
  <span id="freeText14005879102837894290" style="display:none"><b>2020 Re-read </b><br /><br />Urban fantasy is such a great pleasure! I love these tales of werewolves, vampires, fae, and witches, all located in contemporary cities. I'm particularly partial to stories of the fae and vampires. They make such great main characters or wonderful villains. This story gives us both of my favourites as the bad guys, making Charles and Anna work hard to keep this summit meeting on an even keel.<br /><br />Anna gets to show her resilience more than once. Everyone thinks she is a weak creature, but now she has back-up in Charles. More importantly, he is also hers to protect and she'll do whatever is necessary to accomplish that goal. The advantage to being an Omega is that she has all of the dominance without the need for violence. No need, but not prevented from violence. She is coming into her strength.<br /><br />Daniel Dos Santos has redeemed himself with this cover. Someone who didn't know better might mistake it for a Lassie story, but at least Anna is dressed like a real woman and that makes her far sexier than the image on the cover of the first volume. Well done.<br /><br /><b>ORIGINAL REVIEW:</b><br /><br />I think I like this splinter series of Patricia Briggs more than her original Mercy Thompson series. The first Alpha &amp; Omega book annoyed me because it assumed that I knew things that I didn’t. I hadn’t read the short story that kicked things off. But with that in the past, I can appreciate this second book for exactly what it is.<br /><br />I always love urban fantasy that includes the Fae. They are far superior to vampires &amp; werewolves in my reading experience. I’m not sure what it is about the fairy tale aspects that grabs me—maybe it’s my Scandinavian background that makes me love a good troll. And this story contains just enough Fae elements to keep me happy.<br /><br />Then there is Charles and Anna’s relationship. It’s a done deal and it’s working well. There’s none of the “will s/he or won’t s/he” questions that occupied so much time and energy in the first several books of the MT series. This seems to me to be much more interesting—how do two people work out their differences and make a relationship work?<br /><br />A very satisfying urban fantasy and I will definitely be moving on to the third installment soon.</span>
  <a data-text-id="14005879102837894290" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_1887896941" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1887896941" />
    <a title="Sarah" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/3344685-sarah"><img alt="Sarah" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1388694025p2/3344685.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1887896941?book_show_action=true">Jan 22, 2017</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Sarah" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Sarah" href="/user/show/3344685-sarah">Sarah</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Mass Market Paperback 9781841497952" href="/book/show/6124297-hunting-ground">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3344685-sarah?shelf=books-i-own-print">books-i-own-print</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3344685-sarah?shelf=read-in-2018">read-in-2018</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3344685-sarah?shelf=read-in-2017">read-in-2017</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3344685-sarah?shelf=books-i-own-kindle">books-i-own-kindle</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3344685-sarah?shelf=read-in-2014">read-in-2014</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3344685-sarah?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3344685-sarah?shelf=buddy-read">buddy-read</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3344685-sarah?shelf=read-in-2015">read-in-2015</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1887896941" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer1448115773509811220"><b>1st Read March 2014</b><br/><b>2nd Read December 2015</b><br/><b>3rd Read January 2017</b><br/><b>4th Read January 2018</b><br/><br/><b>Original Review</b><br/><br/>I have been absolutely devouring the both the Mercy Thompson and Alpha & Omega series recently so it's no surprise that I enjoyed <b>Hunting Ground</b>. I think I'm just going to love everything that <b>Patricia Briggs</b> writes because she certainly hasn't steered me wrong so far! The world building in these two series is phenomenal, you have the werewolves with their dominance issues, the fae who are very good</span>
  <span id="freeText1448115773509811220" style="display:none"><b>1st Read March 2014</b><br /><b>2nd Read December 2015</b><br /><b>3rd Read January 2017</b><br /><b>4th Read January 2018</b><br /><br /><b>Original Review</b><br /><br />I have been absolutely devouring the both the Mercy Thompson and Alpha &amp; Omega series recently so it's no surprise that I enjoyed <b>Hunting Ground</b>. I think I'm just going to love everything that <b>Patricia Briggs</b> writes because she certainly hasn't steered me wrong so far! The world building in these two series is phenomenal, you have the werewolves with their dominance issues, the fae who are very good at keeping secrets plus of course the vampires have their own agendas and I can't get enough of it all. The Alpha and Omega series gives us a change to discover much more about Pack politics and to see how issues are resolved in the world of the werewolves.<br /><br />Bran has decided that it is time for the werewolves to make their presence known to the general public, he knows that they aren't going to be able to remain hidden for much longer with all this modern technology and he knows it is better to come out on their own terms before they are discovered. As the Alpha who has control of the whole of America Bran doesn't need to ask anyone's permission to carry out his plans but he has agreed to speak to the European werewolves and answer any questions they may have. Charles is the one who gets to be in charge at the conference of Alpha's who have gathered from all over Europe to discuss the issue. It's never easy to have so many Alpha wolves in one place where they're all fighting to prove their dominance but things get even more complicated when some of their visitors come under attack from an unknown enemy. It is up to Charles and Anna to get to the bottom of what is happening before one of them pays the ultimate price.<br /><br />The best thing about the Alpha &amp; Omega books is the relationship development between Anna and Charles. When we met Anna she had been abused and beaten down for years so it is taking time for her to build her confidence. Deep down she knows that Charles would never hurt her but she still scares easily, especially when they are surrounded by Alpha wolves. I have loved seeing them work through things together, neither of them is experienced when it comes to relationships so even though Charles is so much older than Anna is these feelings are new to him too and it is so sweet watching him try to figure things out. What I love most about Charles is the way he protects Anna without being overprotective, he actually encourages her to stand on her own two feet and is there to provide extra support when she needs it. My favourite Charles quote shows exactly what I mean:<br /><br /><i>"If it would benefit you, I would kill every wolf here. But there are things that you need to do - and interfering with that is not protecting, not in my book, the best way for me to protect you is to encourage you to be able to protect yourself."</i><br /><br />Both Anna and Charles are completely out of their comfort zone here which helps them bond with each other on a deeper level than before and grow as a couple. We get to see Anna learn more about her role as Omega and how she fits into the Pack hierarchy. <i>“An Omega wolf is an Alpha wolf who is extremely zen.”</i> That has to be the best description I've ever seen of an Omega and it explains Anna's role perfectly, she has all the protective instincts of an Alpha but is missing the violent tendencies they usually display. That doesn't mean she won't fight to protect her Pack but it does mean violence isn't going to be the first thing she resorts to.<br /><br />The romance may be an important part of this series but <b>Hunting Ground</b> is also an action packed story that has so much going on it will keep you on the edge of your seat from beginning to end. I did manage to figure out who was behind the attacks eventually but not until very near the end of the book and only just before Anna and Charles did. I just couldn't read this book fast enough and it's left me desperate to carry on with the series!<br /><br />________________________________<br /><br /><b>2nd Read</b><br /><br />Buddy read with <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/865983411" rel="nofollow noopener">Ange</a><br /><br />Since it's been nearly 2 years since Ange &amp; I buddy read this series last we decided we're well overdue another read in the run up to the release of Fire Touched next March.<br /><br />I love this series so much! The characters, the world building just everything about these books makes them a comfort read for me. Along with Ilona Andrews's Kate Daniels series this is probably my most reread series &amp; I never get tired of it.<br /><br />________________________________<br /><br /><b>3rd Read</b><br /><br />I'm running out of words of praise for this series. The fact that I'm on my 4th reread of most of the books in this series should give you an idea how much I love it though. Anna and Charles &lt;3&lt;3&lt;3</span>
  <a data-text-id="1448115773509811220" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_106809702" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/106809702" />
    <a title="AH" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/3255548-ah"><img alt="AH" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1275413869p2/3255548.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/106809702?book_show_action=true">Jun 12, 2010</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="AH" class="user" itemprop="url" name="AH" href="/user/show/3255548-ah">AH</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3255548-ah?shelf=own">own</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3255548-ah?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3255548-ah?shelf=witches">witches</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3255548-ah?shelf=were">were</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3255548-ah?shelf=urban-fantasy">urban-fantasy</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3255548-ah?shelf=fae">fae</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3255548-ah?shelf=vampires">vampires</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3255548-ah?shelf=zzread-mar-2011">zzread-mar-2011</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer106809702" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer3263176437280396415">Werewolf politics and intrigue are the highlight of this novel. Charles and Anna are sent to Seattle on behalf of Bran to negotiate the “coming out” of the werewolf population. The wolves of North America and Europe are represented in this negotiation. Not all the wolves are happy with this situation, and a lot of Alpha wolves in one place is a recipe for trouble. The talks are to be mediated by a fae Gray Lord, Dana.<br/><br/>There was a huge cast of characters in this book and it was interesting to lear</span>
  <span id="freeText3263176437280396415" style="display:none">Werewolf politics and intrigue are the highlight of this novel. Charles and Anna are sent to Seattle on behalf of Bran to negotiate the “coming out” of the werewolf population. The wolves of North America and Europe are represented in this negotiation. Not all the wolves are happy with this situation, and a lot of Alpha wolves in one place is a recipe for trouble. The talks are to be mediated by a fae Gray Lord, Dana.<br /><br />There was a huge cast of characters in this book and it was interesting to learn about the wolf packs from different countries. It was a real eye opener to see just how powerful Bran was without him actually being in the story. The interactions between pack Alphas was intriguing, if not on the precipice of violence. I loved how they all seemed to walk on eggshells. I was amused at how a simple Omega wolf could cause a bunch of Alphas to want to rush and rescue her and how she could easily calm them down. <br /><br />This is the book where Anna shines as a character. Still skittish, Anna relies on her wolf nature in order to adjust to situations. Anna is learning how to be an Omega wolf and what it entails. The wolves are also learning the power of an Omega. I loved watching Anna transform from a “scared rabbit” to an assertive, protective wolf. <br /><br />I loved the stolen moments that Anna and Charles shared. Theirs is a strange and unusual relationship: their wolves chose each other as mates. I found it fascinating that Anna allowed her wolf nature to take over during their moments together. It was as if her wolf was protecting her from her past, painful memories. It was also nice to see the tender side of Charles. He was so sweet and patient with Anna. <br /><br />The author has a talent of creating an urban fantasy world that feels so believable. I love to be immersed in this world. I’m just sad that there will be a long wait for the next book<br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="3263176437280396415" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_150073305" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/150073305" />
    <a title="Annie (Under the Covers Book Blog)" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/2489554-annie-under-the-covers-book-blog"><img alt="Annie (Under the Covers Book Blog)" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1352609417p2/2489554.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/150073305?book_show_action=true">Feb 23, 2011</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Annie (Under the Covers Book Blog)" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Annie (Under the Covers Book Blog)" href="/user/show/2489554-annie-under-the-covers-book-blog">Annie (Under the Covers Book Blog)</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>


          <div><span class="uitext greyText">Recommends it for: </span>
           <span class="uitext reviewText">Mercy Thompson fans, Urban Fantasy fans</span></div>

        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2489554-annie-under-the-covers-book-blog?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2489554-annie-under-the-covers-book-blog?shelf=drinks-on-me">drinks-on-me</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2489554-annie-under-the-covers-book-blog?shelf=king-of-the-harem">king-of-the-harem</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2489554-annie-under-the-covers-book-blog?shelf=genre-urban-fantasy">genre-urban-fantasy</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2489554-annie-under-the-covers-book-blog?shelf=vampires">vampires</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2489554-annie-under-the-covers-book-blog?shelf=my-hottie-harem">my-hottie-harem</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2489554-annie-under-the-covers-book-blog?shelf=books-i-go-rabid-over">books-i-go-rabid-over</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2489554-annie-under-the-covers-book-blog?shelf=covers-to-covet">covers-to-covet</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2489554-annie-under-the-covers-book-blog?shelf=read-in-2011">read-in-2011</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2489554-annie-under-the-covers-book-blog?shelf=werewolves">werewolves</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer150073305" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer2201915202104079186">Wow. I didn’t think this series could get any better, but it just did. <i>Hunting Ground</i> was amazing!! I love the way Briggs writes. There’s this ease to it and it’s always just a natural progression of the storyline. It’s never pulling or straining. All the characters continue to grow in a way that is gradual, but still very evident.<br/><br/>And Anna is the perfect example of that. I remember complaining back in the Alpha &Omega novella that she was too skittish and broken. But she has come so far in such </span>
  <span id="freeText2201915202104079186" style="display:none">Wow. I didn’t think this series could get any better, but it just did. <i>Hunting Ground</i> was amazing!! I love the way Briggs writes. There’s this ease to it and it’s always just a natural progression of the storyline. It’s never pulling or straining. All the characters continue to grow in a way that is gradual, but still very evident.<br /><br />And Anna is the perfect example of that. I remember complaining back in the Alpha &amp;Omega novella that she was too skittish and broken. But she has come so far in such a short time and yet it doesn’t seem like she suddenly grew a pair and is capable of manhandling all the Alpha werewolves at once. She’s grown in a gradual way that makes her success at getting over her past a personal accomplishment and one that opens opportunities for her to love someone....someone like Charles.<br /><br />What I love about this series is the romance. It’s not perfect where Anna and Charles find each other and fall desperately in love with each other and they love happily ever after. THE END. No, not here. Both of them are unsure and probably a little scared and that makes the romance between these two all the more interesting. A light touch in human form or a slight nudge in wolf form makes the relationship fascinating because they are learning each other slowly. It’s just great to read.<br /><br />And then there’s all the wolf politics! Wow, I wasn’t expecting half of the twists that Briggs pulled in this one! I was completely taken aback and it was definitely one I’d like to pick up again soon. With all the fae, vampires, and werewolves in this one, I’m sure there’s something there for everyone!<br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="2201915202104079186" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

Just enough clues sprinkled throughout for me to guess some of them and still leave enough mystery to unfold. Plus, enough realism in the human relationship between two lonely,</span>
  <span id="freeText891497390504804882" style="display:none">★★★★★ Wow! All I can say is this book is cool. I just love “Anna Latham Cornick, mate of Charles Cornick, Omega of the Aspen Creek Pack. Wolf. Sister. Daughter. Lover. Beloved.” Remember, knowing a person’s name is powerful magic. And that is all the hint of this plot you are going to get out of me! This one is delicious. Just enough clues sprinkled throughout for me to guess some of them and still leave enough mystery to unfold. Plus, enough realism in the human relationship between two lonely, insecure souls verses their newly established mate-bond to be fascinating. Not to mention, the cover actually looks like Anna and Brother Wolf. Finally.<br><br>Don’t miss the fun. Start this one with the novella to get the full effect. I can’t wait for <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/7942786.Fair_Game__Alpha___Omega___3_" title="Fair Game (Alpha &amp; Omega, #3) by Patricia Briggs" rel="nofollow noopener">Fair Game</a>, coming out February, 2012.<br><br><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/5393637.Alpha___Omega__Alpha___Omega___0_5_" title="Alpha &amp; Omega (Alpha &amp; Omega, #0.5) by Patricia Briggs" rel="nofollow noopener">

<span id="freeTextContainer17384680467881973765">I enjoyed Anna and Charles' story in this book.<br/>Anna may have a long way to go, but she has recovered quite a bit of her spunk. It's nice to see her gain some confidence in herself and in her ability to stand up on her own two feet. I should have known that Briggs wouldn't leave her as a frightened shaking mess. I really like the way that she deals with characters who have been traumatized. She doesn't give them a miracle recovery, they have to slowly work the problems out for themselves over tim</span>
  <span id="freeText17384680467881973765" style="display:none">I enjoyed Anna and Charles' story in this book.<br />Anna may have a long way to go, but she has recovered quite a bit of her spunk. It's nice to see her gain some confidence in herself and in her ability to stand up on her own two feet. I should have known that Briggs wouldn't leave her as a frightened shaking mess. I really like the way that she deals with characters who have been traumatized. She doesn't give them a miracle recovery, they have to slowly work the problems out for themselves over time. <br />Charles is such a suprise to me. I expected him to be a little more gruff and bullheaded since he has been a bachlor for basically 200 years. It's nice to see a strong male character who is secure enough to catch an air kiss! He's whipped, he likes it, and he doesn't care who knows. Then again, I don't think anyone is going to give him a hard time for it.<br /></span>

<span id="freeTextContainer9902021245840353200"><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1472750173i/20237706._SX540_.jpg' width='200' height='150' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><b>Awesome. Just awesome. </b><br/><br/>This was just perfection in an audiobook. The reader, Holter Graham, again slammed-dunked it with a spot on narration. The way he does each voice so distinctly and uniquely and manages to give each sentence the right tone... I just love it. I only want to listen to this series in audiobook. <br/><br/>This is the rare breed of UF with a heroine who is not the least bit annoying. She is strong and drama-free and I could read about her all day long. I liked that the focus of the story </span>
  <span id="freeText9902021245840353200" style="display:none"><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1472750173i/20237706._SX540_.jpg" width="200" height="150" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>Awesome. Just awesome. </b><br><br>This was just perfection in an audiobook. The reader, Holter Graham, again slammed-dunked it with a spot on narration. The way he does each voice so distinctly and uniquely and manages to give each sentence the right tone... I just love it. I only want to listen to this series in audiobook. <br><br>This is the rare breed of UF with a heroine who is not the least bit annoying. She is strong and drama-free and I could read about her all day long. I liked that the focus of the story was on the action and the mystery instead of silly relationship drama (ahem, <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/10765906.The_Shadow_Reader__Shadow_Reader___1_" title="The Shadow Reader (Shadow Reader, #1) by Sandy Williams" rel="nofollow noopener">The Shadow Reader</a>). And the mystery was executed to a T. You know the type, the kind where you have no idea who the bad guy is but when you find out, it all makes perfect sense. Excellent work, Patricia Briggs. <br><br>I'm going to pause here and move on to the Mercy Thompson series because I hear that the next Alpha Omega book takes place farther down the timeline in the Mercy world, and I don't want that series spoiled for me. However, it is going to be hard to leave these characters behind. </span>

    <div class="section">
      

<div id="review_441680141" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/441680141" />
    <a title="Kathleen" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/13954899-kathleen"><img alt="Kathleen" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1365166675p2/13954899.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/441680141?book_show_action=true">Oct 25, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Kathleen" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Kathleen" href="/user/show/13954899-kathleen">Kathleen</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/8130498-hunting-ground">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13954899-kathleen?shelf=magic-fantasy">magic-fantasy</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13954899-kathleen?shelf=fantastical-romance">fantastical-romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13954899-kathleen?shelf=series">series</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer441680141" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer539792160139878284">Tense, fast-paced, and emotionally gripping, <i>Hunting Ground</i> is set in Seattle. First stop, a city landmark: a huge stone troll guarding his turf beneath the Fremont Street underpass. Photos don't do justice to the SIZE of this thing, clutching a real VW Bug in one hand. See troll here: <a target='_blank' rel='noopener nofollow' href='http://openplac.es/trips/the-fremont-troll-in-seattle-wa'>http://openplac.es/trips/the-fremont-...</a><br/><br/><b>CHARACTERS:</b> Charles and Anna and a mix of secondary characters (including Moira and Tom, introduced in the prequel Seeing Eyes, a short story in the <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/6122181.Strange_Brew' title='Strange Brew by P.N. Elrod' rel='nofollow noopener'>Strange Brew</a> anthology).</span>
  <span id="freeText539792160139878284" style="display:none">Tense, fast-paced, and emotionally gripping, <i>Hunting Ground</i> is set in Seattle. First stop, a city landmark: a huge stone troll guarding his turf beneath the Fremont Street underpass. Photos don't do justice to the SIZE of this thing, clutching a real VW Bug in one hand. See troll here: <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://openplac.es/trips/the-fremont-troll-in-seattle-wa">http://openplac.es/trips/the-fremont-...</a><br /><br /><b>CHARACTERS:</b> Charles and Anna and a mix of secondary characters (including Moira and Tom, introduced in the prequel Seeing Eyes, a short story in the <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/6122181.Strange_Brew" title="Strange Brew by P.N. Elrod" rel="nofollow noopener">Strange Brew</a> anthology). There's the wanna-be King Arthur character. The Beast, Chastien. Sunny. The Alpha of the Seattle pack. The Fae Lady. The vampires. Etc. All the characters were marked by internal consistency. Kudos to Briggs.<br /><br /><b>PLOT: </b> Solid. Lots of scary dark magic, with just enough lovin' times (loved the bonding scene on the log at the water's edge). No glaring plot contrivances or absurd improbabilities (beyond the fantasticalツ The plot was coherent and suspenseful. Briggs kept me guessing. I determined the villain eventually, but it was not obvious. Maybe a slow start, but action kicks in soon enough and doesn't let up. I was on the edge of my seat.<br /><br /><b>Omega Kicks Ass: </b>In this book, Briggs further develops Anna's character. The formerly abused omega werewolf has guts as well as wisdom. She's attacked or kidnapped numerous times, but she's always thinking through the various possible scenarios and sleuthing out the villains. I sympathized with protective Charles, especially when he (his brother wolf) was sooo upset after <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ Anna, Moira, and Tom were attacked by vamps on the street, and also when he went after the Beast who threatened Anna, at the pack hunt party. The scene immediately after the pack hunt, at the beach, was sweet, a little poignant, and showed Anna's wisdom. Also enjoyed the scene when Charles went after vampires. LOL. He is ferocious for his Anna!!  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br /><br />But despite all Charles's heroic derring do, in the end, Anna kicks asparagus, too. She's come a long way from the role forced on her in the prequel, <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/5393637.Alpha___Omega__Alpha___Omega___0_5_" title="Alpha &amp; Omega (Alpha &amp; Omega, #0.5) by Patricia Briggs" rel="nofollow noopener">Alpha &amp; Omega: A Companion Novella to Cry Wolf</a>.<br /><br />Note: We learn a little more about their mating bond gifts. Before the Hunt begins ( 62%) Anna shifts faster than the others, and much faster than she could before mating with Charles. It's a gift from Brother Wolf (Charles was born a pup and so he alone can shift instantly.)<br /><br /><b>Minor Gripes: </b> Some redundancy get a bit boring. I am not crazy about how Briggs shows the same scene from multiple POVs, as with the first attack on Anna. We "saw" this attack in present time, when it happened, mainly through Anna's POV. Then, we "saw" it again when Charles came along looking for clues. Then, AGAIN when Anna had to describe the attack to Angus and Charles. This type of thing, along with bouts of introspection. )<br /><br /><b>The A&amp;O series, including two short stories: </b><br /><br />0.5 <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/5393637.Alpha___Omega__Alpha___Omega___0_5_" title="Alpha &amp; Omega (Alpha &amp; Omega, #0.5) by Patricia Briggs" rel="nofollow noopener">Alpha &amp; Omega</a> a novella, prequel <br />1. <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/2355575.Cry_Wolf__Alpha___Omega___1_" title="Cry Wolf (Alpha &amp; Omega, #1) by Patricia Briggs" rel="nofollow noopener">Cry Wolf</a><br />1.5 in the <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/6122181.Strange_Brew" title="Strange Brew by P.N. Elrod" rel="nofollow noopener">Strange Brew</a> anthology (<i>Seeing Eye </i>introduces Tom and Moira, who appear in bk 2.<br />2. <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/5292853.Hunting_Ground__Alpha___Omega___2_" title="Hunting Ground (Alpha &amp; Omega, #2) by Patricia Briggs" rel="nofollow noopener">Hunting Ground</a> set in Seattle<br />3. <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/7942786.Fair_Game__Alpha___Omega___3_" title="Fair Game (Alpha &amp; Omega, #3) by Patricia Briggs" rel="nofollow noopener">Fair Game</a></span>
  <a data-text-id="539792160139878284" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('q38NAL1kkkQhJheF+vkODmJKDuT65rnR930AtEC71a5UL5B68rxpGxLMzGVMF5RvcNKZB7zwbDp5JmdaaFev8Q==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('kTSzuW6FN406k+xWAXxz5DD7sjsFkroPDYThdm5TBN9uZC7DIV3M0gl5N7a3kumFImMl2EOEb+SD34aYRr9+gA==')})
  }

<span id="freeTextContainer1964948292961019585"><i>Librarian Note: There is more than one author in the Goodreads database with this name.</i><br/><br/>Patricia Briggs was born in Butte, Montana, to a children’s librarian who passed on to her kids a love of reading and books. Patricia grew up reading fairy tales and books about horses, and later developed an interest in folklore and history. When she decided to write a book of her own, a fantasy book seemed a n</span>
  <span id="freeText1964948292961019585" style="display:none"><i>Librarian Note: There is more than one author in the Goodreads database with this name.</i><br /><br />Patricia Briggs was born in Butte, Montana, to a children’s librarian who passed on to her kids a love of reading and books. Patricia grew up reading fairy tales and books about horses, and later developed an interest in folklore and history. When she decided to write a book of her own, a fantasy book seemed a natural choice. Patricia graduated from Montana State University with degrees in history and German and she worked for a while as a substitute teacher. Currently, she lives in Montana with her husband, children, and six horses and writes full time, much to the delight of her fans.</span>

            <span class="readable">&ldquo;My grandfather would have loved to have met you," he told her huskily. "He would have called you 'She Moves Trees Out of His Path.' "<br /><br /> She looked lost, but his da laughed. He'd known the old man, too.<br /><br /> "He called me 'He Who Must Run into Trees,'" Charles explained, and in a spirit of honesty, a need for his mate to know who he was, he continued, "or sometimes 'Running Eagle.' "<br /><br /> " 'Running Eagle'?" Anna puzzled it over, frowning at him. "What's wrong with that?"<br /><br /> "Too stupid to fly," murmured his father with a little smile.&rdquo;</span>
